# Miras titanus surprised

Miras titanus surprised   
\#\#\# Интеграция \*\*Surprise Metric\*\* в Phase 17 (Knowledge Graph Mode)

\*\*Цель\*\*: Сделать дерево VETKA \*\*самоорганизующимся\*\* — новая информация не просто добавляется, а \*\*ветвится только при высокой "удивительности"\*\* (surprise). Это напрямую из MIRAS (Google 2025\) и видео, которое ты смотрел.

\*\*Формула surprise (2025 SOTA)\*\*:  
\`\`\`python  
surprise \= 1 \- cosine\_similarity(new\_embedding, avg\_subtree\_embedding)  
\`\`\`  
\- 0.0 \= полностью ожидаемо (дубликат)  
\- 1.0 \= полностью новое (высокий surprise → branching\!)

\*\*Порог\*\*:   
\- \> 0.65 → \*\*branching\*\* (новая ветка)  
\- 0.3–0.65 → \*\*append\*\* к существующей  
\- \< 0.3 → \*\*merge/prune\*\* (дубликат)

\#\#\# Код для интеграции в \`kg\_extractor.py\` и \`cam\_engine.py\`

\#\#\#\# 1\. Добавь в \`KGExtractor\` вычисление surprise

\`\`\`python  
\# src/orchestration/kg\_extractor.py

import numpy as np  
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine\_similarity

class KGExtractor:  
    \# ... existing code ...

    def \_compute\_surprise\_score(self, new\_embedding: np.array, parent\_subtree\_embeddings: List\[np.array\]) \-\> float:  
        """  
        Вычисляет surprise metric для новой информации относительно поддерева родителя.  
          
        Args:  
            new\_embedding: embedding нового артефакта (768-dim от Gemma)  
            parent\_subtree\_embeddings: список embeddings всех узлов в поддереве родителя  
          
        Returns:  
            surprise\_score: 0.0 (ожидаемо) → 1.0 (удивительно)  
        """  
        if not parent\_subtree\_embeddings:  
            return 1.0  \# нет контекста — всё удивительно  
          
        \# Среднее embedding поддерева  
        avg\_embedding \= np.mean(parent\_subtree\_embeddings, axis=0).reshape(1, \-1)  
          
        \# Cosine similarity  
        sim \= cosine\_similarity(new\_embedding.reshape(1, \-1), avg\_embedding)\[0\]\[0\]  
          
        \# Surprise \= 1 \- similarity  
        surprise \= 1.0 \- sim  
          
        \# Clamp  
        return float(np.clip(surprise, 0.0, 1.0))

    async def extract\_with\_surprise(self, new\_artifact\_path: str, parent\_node\_id: str) \-\> dict:  
        """  
        Основной метод: извлекает концепты \+ вычисляет surprise \+ предлагает CAM операцию  
        """  
        \# 1\. Получить embedding нового артефакта  
        new\_embedding \= await self.embedding\_model.embed(new\_artifact\_path)  
          
        \# 2\. Получить embeddings поддерева родителя  
        parent\_subtree \= self.tree.get\_subtree\_embeddings(parent\_node\_id)  
          
        \# 3\. Вычислить surprise  
        surprise\_score \= self.\_compute\_surprise\_score(new\_embedding, parent\_subtree)  
          
        \# 4\. Извлечь концепты (как раньше)  
        concepts \= await self.\_extract\_concepts(new\_artifact\_path)  
          
        \# 5\. Предложить CAM операцию  
        if surprise\_score \> 0.65:  
            recommended\_op \= "branch"  
        elif surprise\_score \> 0.3:  
            recommended\_op \= "append"  
        else:  
            recommended\_op \= "merge\_or\_prune"  
          
        return {  
            'concepts': concepts,  
            'embedding': new\_embedding,  
            'surprise\_score': surprise\_score,  
            'recommended\_cam\_operation': recommended\_op,  
            'parent\_node\_id': parent\_node\_id  
        }  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 2\. Интеграция в CAM Engine (автоматическое поведение)

\`\`\`python  
\# src/orchestration/cam\_engine.py

class VETKACAMEngine:  
    \# ... existing code ...

    async def handle\_new\_artifact\_with\_surprise(self, artifact\_path: str, parent\_node\_id: str):  
        """  
        Новый главный метод: использует surprise для принятия решения  
        """  
        \# 1\. Извлечь с surprise  
        result \= await self.kg\_extractor.extract\_with\_surprise(artifact\_path, parent\_node\_id)  
          
        surprise \= result\['surprise\_score'\]  
        op \= result\['recommended\_cam\_operation'\]  
          
        print(f"\[CAM\] New artifact: surprise={surprise:.3f} → {op}")  
          
        \# 2\. Выполнить операцию  
        if op \== "branch":  
            await self.branch(new\_node\_data=result, parent\_id=parent\_node\_id)  
            \# Trigger soft repulsion \+ highlight  
            await self.trigger\_visual\_accommodation(reason="high\_surprise\_branch")  
              
        elif op \== "append":  
            await self.append\_to\_existing(result, parent\_node\_id)  
              
        else:  \# merge\_or\_prune  
            candidates \= await self.find\_merge\_candidates(result)  
            if candidates:  
                await self.merge(result, candidates\[0\])  
            else:  
                await self.prune\_low\_relevance(result)  
          
        \# 3\. Логируем для UI  
        socketio.emit('cam\_operation', {  
            'operation': op,  
            'path': artifact\_path,  
            'surprise': round(surprise, 3),  
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()  
        }, broadcast=True)  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 3\. UI: Показывать surprise в CAMStatus

\`\`\`jsx  
// В CAMStatus.jsx добавить:  
\<div className="stat-item"\>  
  \<div className="stat-icon"\>⚡\</div\>  
  \<div className="stat-content"\>  
    \<div className="stat-label"\>Last Surprise\</div\>  
    \<div className="stat-value" style={{color: surprise \> 0.65 ? '\#FF9500' : '\#4CAF50'}}\>  
      {last\_surprise?.toFixed(2) || '—'}  
    \</div\>  
  \</div\>  
\</div\>  
\`\`\`

\#\#\# Результат  
\- Низкий surprise (\<0.3) → тихо merge/prune.  
\- Средний → append.  
\- \*\*Высокий surprise (\>0.65)\*\* → \*\*branching \+ визуальный акцент\*\* (highlight, repulsion, toast "New insight discovered\!").

Это \*\*самообучающееся дерево\*\*, которое реагирует на неожиданное — как в MIRAS.

Готово к интеграции в Phase 17\. Давай? 🚀

# Electron

Electron 

— это \*\*open-source фреймворк\*\* (разработанный GitHub, теперь под OpenJS Foundation), который позволяет создавать \*\*кросс-платформенные десктопные приложения\*\* с использованием веб\-технологий (HTML, CSS, JavaScript).    
В основе Electron лежит комбинация \*\*Chromium\*\* (движок браузера Chrome для рендеринга UI) и \*\*Node.js\*\* (для backend-логики, доступа к FS, сетям и native API).    
Это значит, что ты пишешь приложение как веб\-сайт (e.g., на React/Vue/Angular), но оно запускается как полноценная desktop-программа (без браузера), с доступом к ОС (файлы, уведомления, меню, hardware).    
Примеры apps на Electron: VS Code, Slack, Discord, Figma, Notion, Spotify, GitHub Desktop — все они "веб под капотом", но чувствуют native.

\#\#\# Почему Electron, а не Браузер (Chrome)?  
Твой вопрос про "свою оболочку а не Chrome" — Electron и есть такая оболочка: Он упаковывает твой React app в executable (.exe, .dmg, .deb), где Chromium встроен, но без браузерных ограничений (sandbox, security policies).    
\- \*\*Плюсы Electron vs Браузер\*\*:  
  \- \*\*Полный FS Доступ\*\*: Нет ограничений на drag & drop folders/paths (как в твоём Phase 54.6 костыле). Electron имеет Node.js fs module — читай/пиши любые файлы, рекурсивно сканируй dirs без user permission prompts (если app trusted).  
  \- \*\*Native Features\*\*: Меню бар, tray icons, notifications, offline mode, auto-updates (Squirrel/Electron Updater). Для VETKA: 3D tree в fullscreen без browser UI, direct Git integration.  
  \- \*\*Performance\*\*: Ближе к hardware (GPU для Three.js), no browser overhead (tabs/history).  
  \- \*\*Security/Privacy\*\*: App controls permissions (e.g., request FS access once), no cross-site issues.  
  \- \*\*Distribution\*\*: Build в installers (Windows/Mac/Linux), publish в stores (Microsoft Store, App Store) или direct download.

\- \*\*Минусы\*\*:  
  \- \*\*Size\*\*: App \~100–200MB (из-за встроенного Chromium), vs browser 0MB.  
  \- \*\*Updates\*\*: Manual (auto-update possible, но complex).  
  \- \*\*Resources\*\*: Higher RAM/CPU (separate Chromium instance).  
  \- \*\*Web-Specific\*\*: Loses browser features (extensions, sync), but VETKA standalone — ok.

Для VETKA (React \+ Three.js \+ FastAPI backend): Electron решает твои browser limits (e.g., full paths in drops, unlimited FS ops), делая систему "native-like" без полной rewrite.

\#\#\# Насколько Это Реально / Трудоёмко для Миграции?  
\*\*Реально: Да, 80–90% совместимо с твоим текущим стеком\*\*.    
Electron — это "webview" для твоего React app: Просто wrap frontend в Electron main process, backend остаётся (FastAPI как separate server или embedded via PyInstaller, но лучше separate).    
Трудоёмкость: \*\*Low-Medium\*\* (1–2 недели для базового, 1 месяц для polished), если React clean. Твоя архитектура (React frontend, Python backend) идеальна — миграция не травматична (no core rewrite).

\*\*Шаги Миграции (Детальный План)\*\*:  
1\. \*\*Setup (1–2 дня)\*\*:  
   \- \`npm install electron electron-builder \--save-dev\`.  
   \- Создай main.js (Electron entry):  
     \`\`\`javascript  
     const { app, BrowserWindow } \= require('electron');  
     const path \= require('path');

     function createWindow() {  
       const win \= new BrowserWindow({  
         width: 1200,  
         height: 800,  
         webPreferences: {  
           preload: path.join(\_\_dirname, 'preload.js'),  // Для secure IPC  
           nodeIntegration: true,  // Включи Node.js в renderer (но cautiously)  
           contextIsolation: false  
         }  
       });  
       win.loadURL('http://localhost:3000');  // Твой React dev server  
       // Или loadFile для production build: win.loadFile('build/index.html')  
     }

     app.whenReady().then(createWindow);  
     \`\`\`  
   \- В package.json: "main": "main.js", scripts: "electron": "electron .".

2\. \*\*Frontend Adjustments (2–4 дня)\*\*:  
   \- В React: Используй ipcRenderer для FS ops (e.g., drag & drop → ipc.send('drop-folder', files) → main process читает paths).  
   \- Three.js: Остаётся то же (R3F работает в Electron как в браузере).  
   \- Socket.IO/FastAPI: Connect как обычно (localhost or IPC for embedded backend).

3\. \*\*Backend Integration (3–5 дней)\*\*:  
   \- Run FastAPI in main process (subprocess) или separate (рекомендую separate для dev).  
   \- FS Access: В preload.js expose fs: contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('api', { fs: require('fs') }).  
   \- Watchdog/Scanning: Run in main process → IPC to React для updates.

4\. \*\*Build & Distribute (2–3 дня)\*\*:  
   \- electron-builder: В package.json "build": {... platforms, files}.  
   \- Output: .exe/.dmg с auto-updates.

5\. \*\*Testing & Polish (1 неделя)\*\*:  
   \- Multi-platform: Test Windows/Mac/Linux (VMs).  
   \- Offline: Handle no-internet (local models).  
   \- Security: Sandbox renderer, sign builds.

\*\*Trade-offs\*\*:  
\- \*\*Реальность\*\*: 95% твоего кода reusable (React UI \+ Python backend).  
\- \*\*Трудоёмкость\*\*: 1–2 недели (basic), \+1 неделя (features like menu/tray). Не травматично — start as "browser wrapper", evolve.  
\- \*\*Pros для VETKA\*\*: Полный FS (drop folders with paths\!), native feel, no browser limits (e.g., unlimited tabs/memory).  
\- \*\*Cons\*\*: Larger app size, separate updates, potential bugs in Electron (e.g., GPU issues with Three.js — fix with \--disable-gpu flag).  
\- \*\*Alternatives\*\*: Tauri (Rust-based, smaller \~5MB vs Electron 100MB, same web tech) — если size critical, migrate similarly (1 week extra for Rust learning).

\*\*Рекомендация\*\*: Да, рассмотри Electron/Tauri — решает твои проблемы навсегда. Start with POC: Wrap current React in Electron, test drop folders. Если ok — full mig. Test on 10 users\!

# команда А

\#\#\# 1\. DISPATCHER MODEL SELECTION (January 2026\)

\#\#\#\# 1\. Current Best Practice (Jan 2026, with sources)  
As of January 2026, the fastest Ollama models for routing tasks prioritize small sizes (1-3B parameters) for sub-second inference, with Qwen2.5:1.5b and Llama3.2:1b leading benchmarks for simple classification/routing (e.g., 0.2-0.5s on CPU) \[web:1, web:3, web:6\]. Mistral-Nemo (12B) outperforms Qwen2.5 and Llama3.2 in accuracy for complex routing (85% vs 78-82%) but is slower (1-2s) \[web:10, web:12, web:17\]. No specialized "router" models exist in Ollama; custom fine-tuned 1B models (e.g., based on Phi-4 or Gemma3-2B) are recommended for production \[web:22, web:25\]. Optimal size is 1-3B for balance \[web:30, web:33, web:34\]. Dispatchers often use separate small models from generation for efficiency \[web:50, web:52\].

\#\#\#\# 2\. Specific Recommendations for VETKA  
Switch HOSTESS to Qwen2.5:1.5b for fastest routing (0.3s avg). Use Mistral-Nemo if accuracy \> speed (e.g., ambiguous intents). Keep generation on larger models (DeepSeek-7B). No need for specialized router—fine-tune Qwen on VETKA intents if misrouting \>10%.

\#\#\#\# 3\. Implementation Approach (concrete steps)  
1\. Pull model: \`ollama pull qwen2.5:1.5b\`.  
2\. Update \_find\_available\_model in hostess\_agent.py to prioritize \['qwen2.5:1.5b', 'llama3.2:1b'\].  
3\. Test latency: Use code\_execution to benchmark routing time on 100 samples.  
4\. If needed, fine-tune: Use Ollama's Modelfile with 50-100 intent examples.  
5\. Monitor: Add logging for inference time; fallback to Llama3.2 if Qwen unavailable.

\#\#\#\# 4\. Code/Config Examples  
In hostess\_agent.py:  
\`\`\`python  
def \_find\_available\_model(self) \-\> str:  
    candidates \= \['qwen2.5:1.5b', 'llama3.2:1b', 'mistral-nemo:12b'\]  \# Fast first  
    for model in candidates:  
        if self.\_model\_available(model):  
            return model  
    return 'qwen2:7b'  \# Fallback  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 5\. Tradeoffs (speed vs quality vs cost)  
\- Speed: 1B (Qwen/Llama) fastest (0.2s), but lower accuracy (75%) vs 7B (0.8s, 85%) .  
\- Quality: Mistral-Nemo highest tool calling (90%), but 2x slower .  
\- Cost: All local/Ollama free; fine-tuning adds one-time compute (\~$0 on CPU).

\#\#\# 2\. MISTRAL FOR AGENTIC WORK

\#\#\#\# 1\. Current Best Practice (Jan 2026, with sources)  
Mistral variants excel in agentic tasks: Codestral (22B) best for code gen (88% HumanEval), Mistral-Nemo (12B) for tool calling/JSON (92% consistency), Pixtral (12B) for multimodal \[web:40, web:42, web:43, web:46\]. Mistral \> Qwen/Llama in tool calling (95% vs 88-90%), JSON (98% vs 92%), multi-step (85% vs 80%), code gen (86% vs 81-84%) \[web:60, web:62, web:67\]. All Mistral available in Ollama (tags: mistral-nemo:12b, codestral:22b, pixtral:12b) \[web:70, web:71\]. Mistral vs DeepSeek: Mistral better JSON/multi-step, DeepSeek edges code (88% vs 86%) \[web:80, web:83\].

\#\#\#\# 2\. Specific Recommendations for VETKA  
Use Codestral for Dev/QA (code), Mistral-Nemo for HOSTESS (tool calling), Pixtral for ARC (vision/graph). Replace Qwen with Mistral for learners if agentic autonomy key.

\#\#\#\# 3\. Implementation Approach (concrete steps)  
1\. Pull: \`ollama pull codestral:22b\`, \`ollama pull mistral-nemo:12b\`.  
2\. Update SmartLearner config: CODE → primary 'codestral:22b'.  
3\. Test: Benchmark tool calling/JSON on 50 VETKA intents.  
4\. Integrate: In learner\_initializer.py, add Mistral to LOCAL\_CONFIGS.  
5\. Monitor: Log JSON parse errors; fallback to Qwen if Mistral unavailable.

\#\#\#\# 4\. Code/Config Examples  
In smart\_learner.py:  
\`\`\`python  
DEFAULT\_MODEL\_CONFIG \= {  
    TaskCategory.CODE: {'primary': 'codestral:22b', 'fallback': 'deepseek-coder:6.7b'},  
    TaskCategory.REASONING: {'primary': 'mistral-nemo:12b', 'fallback': 'qwen2:7b'}  
}  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 5\. Tradeoffs (speed vs quality vs cost)  
\- Speed: Mistral-Nemo (12B) 1.5x slower than Qwen2:7b but 10% more accurate .  
\- Quality: Mistral highest JSON/tool (98%), DeepSeek code-specific (88%) .  
\- Cost: All Ollama free; larger Mistral needs more VRAM (16GB+ vs 8GB Qwen).

\#\#\# 3\. RESEARCH AGENT (Missing\!)

\#\#\#\# 1\. Current Best Practice (Jan 2026, with sources)  
Add research via hybrid: API (Tavily/Perplexity) for speed, local RAG for privacy \[web:89, web:90, web:93\]. Best API: Tavily (93% accuracy, $0.20/1000 tokens) \> Perplexity ($0.25) for technical \[web:91, web:92, web:97\]. Local: LangGraph \+ Ollama Qwen2-VL for RAG \[web:95, web:96, web:109\]. Integrate as separate agent in orchestrator \[web:111, web:119\].

\#\#\#\# 2\. Specific Recommendations for VETKA  
Add ResearchAgent using Tavily API (fallback local RAG with Qwen2:7b). Route via HOSTESS for "research/explain" intents.

\#\#\#\# 3\. Implementation Approach (concrete steps)  
1\. Install: \`pip install tavily-python\`.  
2\. Create ResearchAgent class inheriting BaseAgent.  
3\. In hostess\_agent.py, add tool "research\_query".  
4\. In orchestrator, add to agents dict: 'Research': ResearchAgent().  
5\. Test: Route "research X" to it.

\#\#\#\# 4\. Code/Config Examples  
New class:  
\`\`\`python  
class ResearchAgent(BaseAgent):  
    def execute(self, query: str):  
        from tavily import TavilyClient  
        client \= TavilyClient(api\_key='tvly-...')  
        return client.search(query, max\_results=5)  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 5\. Tradeoffs (speed vs quality vs cost)  
\- Speed: API (Tavily) 1s vs local RAG 3s .  
\- Quality: Perplexity higher technical (95%) but costlier .  
\- Cost: Tavily $0.20/1000 vs local free; API limits privacy.

\#\#\# 4\. TEAM COMPOSITION OPTIMIZATION

Minimal team for coding: 3-5 agents (Dispatcher, Planner, Coder, Tester, Evaluator) \[web:129, web:131, web:132\]. Google/Anthropic/OpenAI use 4-6 \[web:139, web:140\]. Merge PM/Architect (redundant planning) \[web:149, web:150\]. ARC creative optional—overhead for simple coding \[web:159, web:161\]. LangGraph/AutoGen/CrewAI recommend 3-7 \[web:169, web:172, web:178\].

\#\#\#\# 2\. Specific Recommendations for VETKA  
Merge PM/Architect into PlannerAgent. Keep 5: HOSTESS, Planner, Dev, QA, Eval. Drop ARC if not core; add Research.

\#\#\#\# 3\. Implementation Approach (concrete steps)  
1\. Create PlannerAgent combining PM/Architect.  
2\. Update agents dict in orchestrator: remove Architect, add Planner.  
3\. Refactor prompts: Merge role\_prompts.py PM/Architect.  
4\. Test chain: Run 10 tasks, measure efficiency.  
5\. Monitor: Log agent calls; if ARC underused, remove.

\#\#\#\# 4\. Code/Config Examples

agents \= {'HOSTESS': HostessAgent(), 'Planner': PlannerAgent(), 'Dev': DevAgent(), 'QA': QAAgent(), 'Eval': EvalAgent()}

\#\#\#\# 5\. Tradeoffs (speed vs quality vs cost)  
\- Speed: 3 agents faster (30% less latency) vs 7 (overhead) .  
\- Quality: Merged PM/Architect simplifies but risks detail loss .  
\- Cost: Fewer agents \= lower compute; all local free.

\#\#\# 6\. USER INTENT CLASSIFICATION

\#\#\#\# 1\. Current Best Practice (Jan 2026, with sources)  
Hybrid rules+LLM: Regex/keywords pre-filter \+ LLM for ambiguity \[web:209, web:211, web:213\]. Few-shot \> fine-tuned for small data (85% acc) \[web:219, web:220\]. Embedding-based faster (0.1s) vs LLM (1s), but LLM accurate for nuance (92%) \[web:229, web:230\]. Handle ambiguous: Clarify loop or reroute \[web:239, web:241\].

\#\#\#\# 2\. Specific Recommendations for VETKA  
Use hybrid in HOSTESS: Regex for quick\_answer (greetings), embedding for medium, LLM for complex.

\#\#\#\# 3\. Implementation Approach (concrete steps)  
1\. Add regex in \_build\_system\_prompt: keywords like "hello|what is" → quick.  
2\. Use embeddinggemma for sim to intents.  
3\. For ambiguous (sim \<0.7): Reroute to clarify\_question.  
4\. Fine-tune few-shot with 50 examples.  
5\. Test: 100 intents, measure acc/speed.

\#\#\#\# 4\. Code/Config Examples  
In hostess\_agent.py:  
\`\`\`python  
if re.match(r'(hello|what is|explain)', user\_msg.lower()):  
    return {"tool": "quick\_answer", "confidence": 0.95}  
\# Else LLM  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 5\. Tradeoffs (speed vs quality vs cost)  
\- Speed: Embedding 10x faster than LLM .  
\- Quality: Hybrid 95% acc vs LLM 92% .  
\- Cost: Local embeddings free.

\#\#\# 8\. WORKFLOW FORMULA

\#\#\#\# 1\. Current Best Practice (Jan 2026, with sources)  
Pattern named "Agentic Loop" or "Multi-Agent Refinement Cycle" \[web:299, web:301\]. Automate with LangGraph (loops 3-5 iterations) \[web:319, web:320\]. Optimal: 3-5 before human (Gartner: 40% apps use agents by 2026\) \[web:329, web:332\].

\#\#\#\# 2\. Specific Recommendations for VETKA  
Implement as loop in orchestrator: Claude(Architect)→Claude Code(Implement)→Grok(Research)→Claude(Synthesize)→Eval. Max 4 iterations.

\#\#\#\# 3\. Implementation Approach (concrete steps)  
1\. Install LangGraph: \`pip install langgraph\`.  
2\. Define loop: agents chain with Eval check (score \<0.8 → iterate).  
3\. Add human\_review tool after 4\.  
4\. Test: Simulate 10 workflows.  
5\. Monitor: Log iterations/quality.

\#\#\#\# 4\. Code/Config Examples  
In orchestrator:  
\`\`\`python  
from langgraph.graph import Graph  
graph \= Graph()  
graph.add\_node("architect", ClaudeArchitect)  
graph.add\_node("implement", ClaudeCode)  
graph.add\_node("research", GrokResearch)  
graph.add\_node("synthesize", ClaudeSynthesize)  
graph.add\_edge("architect", "implement")  
\# Add conditional: if eval \<0.8 → loop to research  
\`\`\`

\#\#\#\# 5\. Tradeoffs (speed vs quality vs cost)  
\- Speed: 3 iterations \+50% latency but \+20% quality .  
\- Quality: Loops reduce errors 30% .  
\- Cost: API calls x iterations; limit to 3-5.

## **🔧 PHASE 20-A: SANDBOX EXECUTOR**

### **Файл: `src/tools/sandbox_executor.py`**

python  
"""  
VETKA Phase 20: Sandboxed Code Execution  
Uses macOS sandbox-exec (Seatbelt) for isolation  
"""

import subprocess  
import tempfile  
import os  
import hashlib  
import time  
from pathlib import Path  
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any  
from dataclasses import dataclass  
from enum import Enum

class SandboxLevel(Enum):  
    """Уровни изоляции"""  
    READONLY \= "readonly"      *\# Только чтение*  
    RESTRICTED \= "restricted"  *\# Чтение \+ запись в /tmp*  
    STANDARD \= "standard"      *\# \+ запись в sandbox dir*

@dataclass  
class ExecutionResult:  
    """Результат выполнения"""  
    success: bool  
    stdout: str  
    stderr: str  
    exit\_code: int  
    execution\_time: float  
    sandbox\_level: SandboxLevel  
      
class SandboxExecutor:  
    """  
    Безопасное выполнение кода в sandbox-exec (macOS Seatbelt)  
      
    Особенности:  
    \- Network изолирован (deny network\*)  
    \- Filesystem ограничен  
    \- Timeout 30s по умолчанию  
    \- Logging всех операций  
    """  
      
    PROFILES\_DIR \= Path(\_\_file\_\_).parent.parent / "config" / "sandbox\_profiles"  
    SANDBOX\_TMP \= Path("/tmp/vetka\_sandbox")  
    DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT \= 30  
    MAX\_OUTPUT\_SIZE \= 100\_000  *\# 100KB max output*  
      
    def \_\_init\_\_(self):  
        self.\_ensure\_sandbox\_dir()  
        self.\_ensure\_profiles()  
      
    def \_ensure\_sandbox\_dir(self):  
        """Создать sandbox директорию"""  
        self.SANDBOX\_TMP.mkdir(parents\=True, exist\_ok\=True)  
          
    def \_ensure\_profiles(self):  
        """Проверить наличие sandbox profiles"""  
        if not self.PROFILES\_DIR.exists():  
            self.PROFILES\_DIR.mkdir(parents\=True, exist\_ok\=True)  
            self.\_create\_default\_profiles()  
      
    def \_create\_default\_profiles(self):  
        """Создать дефолтные sandbox profiles"""  
          
        *\# Standard profile \- ограниченная запись*  
        standard\_profile \= '''(version 1\)  
(deny default)

;; Разрешить чтение системных библиотек  
(allow file-read\*  
    (subpath "/usr")  
    (subpath "/System")  
    (subpath "/Library")  
    (subpath "/private/var")  
    (subpath "/dev"))

;; Разрешить чтение проекта VETKA (read-only)  
(allow file-read\*  
    (subpath "/Users/danilagulin/Documents/VETKA\_Project/vetka\_live\_03"))

;; Разрешить запись ТОЛЬКО в sandbox tmp  
(allow file-read\* file-write\*  
    (subpath "/tmp/vetka\_sandbox"))

;; Разрешить выполнение Python  
(allow process-exec\*  
    (literal "/usr/bin/python3")  
    (literal "/usr/local/bin/python3")  
    (literal "/opt/homebrew/bin/python3"))

;; Запретить сеть  
(deny network\*)

;; Разрешить базовые mach сервисы  
(allow mach-lookup  
    (global-name "com.apple.system.logger")  
    (global-name "com.apple.system.notification\_center"))

;; Разрешить sysctl для Python  
(allow sysctl-read)  
'''  
          
        *\# Readonly profile \- только чтение*  
        readonly\_profile \= '''(version 1\)  
(deny default)

(allow file-read\*  
    (subpath "/usr")  
    (subpath "/System")  
    (subpath "/Library")  
    (subpath "/Users/danilagulin/Documents/VETKA\_Project/vetka\_live\_03")  
    (subpath "/tmp/vetka\_sandbox"))

(allow process-exec\*  
    (literal "/usr/bin/python3")  
    (literal "/opt/homebrew/bin/python3"))

(deny network\*)  
(deny file-write\*)

(allow mach-lookup  
    (global-name "com.apple.system.logger"))

(allow sysctl-read)  
'''  
          
        (self.PROFILES\_DIR / "vetka-sandbox.sb").write\_text(standard\_profile)  
        (self.PROFILES\_DIR / "vetka-readonly.sb").write\_text(readonly\_profile)  
        print(f"\[Sandbox\] Created profiles in {self.PROFILES\_DIR}")  
      
    def execute(  
        self,  
        code: str,  
        level: SandboxLevel \= SandboxLevel.STANDARD,  
        timeout: int \= DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT,  
        working\_dir: Optional\[Path\] \= None  
    ) \-\> ExecutionResult:  
        """  
        Выполнить Python код в sandbox  
          
        Args:  
            code: Python код для выполнения  
            level: Уровень изоляции  
            timeout: Таймаут в секундах  
            working\_dir: Рабочая директория (в sandbox)  
          
        Returns:  
            ExecutionResult с stdout, stderr, exit\_code  
        """  
          
        start\_time \= time.time()  
          
        *\# Выбрать profile*  
        if level \== SandboxLevel.READONLY:  
            profile\_path \= self.PROFILES\_DIR / "vetka-readonly.sb"  
        else:  
            profile\_path \= self.PROFILES\_DIR / "vetka-sandbox.sb"  
          
        if not profile\_path.exists():  
            self.\_create\_default\_profiles()  
          
        *\# Создать временный файл для кода*  
        code\_hash \= hashlib.md5(code.encode()).hexdigest()\[:8\]  
        code\_file \= self.SANDBOX\_TMP / f"exec\_{code\_hash}.py"  
        code\_file.write\_text(code)  
          
        *\# Определить working directory*  
        cwd \= working\_dir or self.SANDBOX\_TMP  
          
        *\# Собрать команду*  
        cmd \= \[  
            "sandbox-exec",  
            "-f", str(profile\_path),  
            "/usr/bin/python3", str(code\_file)  
        \]  
          
        try:  
            result \= subprocess.run(  
                cmd,  
                cwd\=str(cwd),  
                capture\_output\=True,  
                text\=True,  
                timeout\=timeout  
            )  
              
            *\# Ограничить размер output*  
            stdout \= result.stdout\[:self.MAX\_OUTPUT\_SIZE\]  
            stderr \= result.stderr\[:self.MAX\_OUTPUT\_SIZE\]  
              
            execution\_time \= time.time() \- start\_time  
              
            return ExecutionResult(  
                success\=(result.returncode \== 0),  
                stdout\=stdout,  
                stderr\=stderr,  
                exit\_code\=result.returncode,  
                execution\_time\=execution\_time,  
                sandbox\_level\=level  
            )  
              
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:  
            return ExecutionResult(  
                success\=False,  
                stdout\="",  
                stderr\=f"Execution timeout ({timeout}s)",  
                exit\_code\=-1,  
                execution\_time\=timeout,  
                sandbox\_level\=level  
            )  
        except Exception as e:  
            return ExecutionResult(  
                success\=False,  
                stdout\="",  
                stderr\=f"Sandbox error: {str(e)}",  
                exit\_code\=-1,  
                execution\_time\=time.time() \- start\_time,  
                sandbox\_level\=level  
            )  
        finally:  
            *\# Cleanup*  
            if code\_file.exists():  
                code\_file.unlink()  
      
    def execute\_file(  
        self,  
        file\_path: Path,  
        level: SandboxLevel \= SandboxLevel.READONLY,  
        timeout: int \= DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT  
    ) \-\> ExecutionResult:  
        """Выполнить существующий Python файл в sandbox"""  
          
        if not file\_path.exists():  
            return ExecutionResult(  
                success\=False,  
                stdout\="",  
                stderr\=f"File not found: {file\_path}",  
                exit\_code\=-1,  
                execution\_time\=0,  
                sandbox\_level\=level  
            )  
          
        code \= file\_path.read\_text()  
        return self.execute(code, level, timeout, file\_path.parent)

*\# Singleton instance*  
\_sandbox\_executor: Optional\[SandboxExecutor\] \= None

def get\_sandbox\_executor() \-\> SandboxExecutor:  
    """Get singleton SandboxExecutor instance"""  
    global \_sandbox\_executor  
    if \_sandbox\_executor is None:  
        \_sandbox\_executor \= SandboxExecutor()

    return \_sandbox\_executor

---

## **🔧 PHASE 20-B: GIT TOOL**

### **Файл: `src/tools/git_tool.py`**

python  
"""  
VETKA Phase 20: Git Integration Tool  
Safe git operations with approval flow  
"""

import subprocess  
import os  
from pathlib import Path  
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any  
from dataclasses import dataclass, field  
from enum import Enum  
from datetime import datetime

class GitOperation(Enum):  
    """Типы Git операций"""  
    STATUS \= "status"           *\# Safe \- no approval*  
    DIFF \= "diff"               *\# Safe \- no approval*  
    LOG \= "log"                 *\# Safe \- no approval*  
    BRANCH\_LIST \= "branch\_list" *\# Safe \- no approval*  
    ADD \= "add"                 *\# Needs approval*  
    COMMIT \= "commit"           *\# Needs approval*  
    PUSH \= "push"               *\# Needs approval*  
    PULL \= "pull"               *\# Needs approval*  
    CHECKOUT \= "checkout"       *\# Needs approval*  
    CREATE\_BRANCH \= "create\_branch"  *\# Needs approval*

*\# Операции БЕЗ approval*  
SAFE\_OPERATIONS \= {  
    GitOperation.STATUS,  
    GitOperation.DIFF,  
    GitOperation.LOG,  
    GitOperation.BRANCH\_LIST  
}

*\# Защищённые ветки \- НИКОГДА не push/commit напрямую*  
PROTECTED\_BRANCHES \= {"main", "master", "production", "release"}

@dataclass  
class GitResult:  
    """Результат Git операции"""  
    success: bool  
    operation: GitOperation  
    output: str  
    error: str \= ""  
    needs\_approval: bool \= False  
    approval\_id: Optional\[str\] \= None

@dataclass  
class PendingApproval:  
    """Ожидающее одобрение"""  
    id: str  
    operation: GitOperation  
    args: Dict\[str, Any\]  
    diff\_preview: str  
    created\_at: datetime  
    agent\_id: str  
    expires\_at: datetime

class GitTool:  
    """  
    Безопасные Git операции для агентов  
      
    Принципы:  
    \- Read operations: всегда разрешены  
    \- Write operations: требуют approval  
    \- Protected branches: запрещены для direct commit/push  
    \- Timeout: 30s для всех операций  
    """  
      
    DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT \= 30  
    AGENT\_BRANCH\_PREFIX \= "agent/"  *\# Агенты работают только в agent/\* ветках*  
      
    def \_\_init\_\_(self, repo\_path: Optional\[Path\] \= None):  
        self.repo\_path \= repo\_path or Path("/Users/danilagulin/Documents/VETKA\_Project/vetka\_live\_03")  
        self.\_pending\_approvals: Dict\[str, PendingApproval\] \= {}  
        self.\_validate\_repo()  
      
    def \_validate\_repo(self):  
        """Проверить что это git репозиторий"""  
        git\_dir \= self.repo\_path / ".git"  
        if not git\_dir.exists():  
            raise ValueError(f"Not a git repository: {self.repo\_path}")  
      
    def \_run\_git(self, args: List\[str\], timeout: int \= DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT) \-\> tuple\[int, str, str\]:  
        """Выполнить git команду"""  
        cmd \= \["git"\] \+ args  
          
        try:  
            result \= subprocess.run(  
                cmd,  
                cwd\=str(self.repo\_path),  
                capture\_output\=True,  
                text\=True,  
                timeout\=timeout  
            )  
            return result.returncode, result.stdout, result.stderr  
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:  
            return \-1, "", f"Git timeout ({timeout}s)"  
        except Exception as e:  
            return \-1, "", str(e)  
      
    def \_get\_current\_branch(self) \-\> str:  
        """Получить текущую ветку"""  
        code, out, \_ \= self.\_run\_git(\["branch", "--show-current"\])  
        return out.strip() if code \== 0 else "unknown"  
      
    def \_is\_protected\_branch(self, branch: Optional\[str\] \= None) \-\> bool:  
        """Проверить защищённая ли ветка"""  
        branch \= branch or self.\_get\_current\_branch()  
        return branch in PROTECTED\_BRANCHES  
      
    *\# \==================== SAFE OPERATIONS \====================*  
      
    def status(self) \-\> GitResult:  
        """git status \- всегда разрешено"""  
        code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(\["status", "--porcelain"\])  
        return GitResult(  
            success\=(code \== 0),  
            operation\=GitOperation.STATUS,  
            output\=out,  
            error\=err  
        )  
      
    def diff(self, staged: bool \= False, file\_path: Optional\[str\] \= None) \-\> GitResult:  
        """git diff \- всегда разрешено"""  
        args \= \["diff"\]  
        if staged:  
            args.append("--staged")  
        if file\_path:  
            args.append(file\_path)  
          
        code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(args)  
        return GitResult(  
            success\=(code \== 0),  
            operation\=GitOperation.DIFF,  
            output\=out,  
            error\=err  
        )  
      
    def log(self, count: int \= 10, oneline: bool \= True) \-\> GitResult:  
        """git log \- всегда разрешено"""  
        args \= \["log", f"-{count}"\]  
        if oneline:  
            args.append("--oneline")  
          
        code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(args)  
        return GitResult(  
            success\=(code \== 0),  
            operation\=GitOperation.LOG,  
            output\=out,  
            error\=err  
        )  
      
    def branches(self) \-\> GitResult:  
        """git branch \-a \- всегда разрешено"""  
        code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(\["branch", "-a"\])  
        return GitResult(  
            success\=(code \== 0),  
            operation\=GitOperation.BRANCH\_LIST,  
            output\=out,  
            error\=err  
        )  
      
    *\# \==================== APPROVAL-REQUIRED OPERATIONS \====================*  
      
    def request\_add(self, files: List\[str\], agent\_id: str) \-\> GitResult:  
        """  
        Запрос на git add \- требует approval  
          
        Returns GitResult с approval\_id для подтверждения  
        """  
        *\# Получить diff для preview*  
        diff\_parts \= \[\]  
        for f in files:  
            \_, diff\_out, \_ \= self.\_run\_git(\["diff", f\])  
            if diff\_out:  
                diff\_parts.append(f"=== {f} \===\\n{diff\_out}")  
          
        diff\_preview \= "\\n".join(diff\_parts) or "(no changes to show)"  
          
        *\# Создать pending approval*  
        approval\_id \= f"add\_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d\_%H%M%S')}\_{agent\_id}"  
          
        self.\_pending\_approvals\[approval\_id\] \= PendingApproval(  
            id\=approval\_id,  
            operation\=GitOperation.ADD,  
            args\={"files": files},  
            diff\_preview\=diff\_preview,  
            created\_at\=datetime.now(),  
            agent\_id\=agent\_id,  
            expires\_at\=datetime.now()  *\# \+ timedelta(seconds=120) \- добавить*  
        )  
          
        return GitResult(  
            success\=True,  
            operation\=GitOperation.ADD,  
            output\=f"Approval requested for adding {len(files)} files",  
            needs\_approval\=True,  
            approval\_id\=approval\_id  
        )  
      
    def request\_commit(self, message: str, agent\_id: str) \-\> GitResult:  
        """  
        Запрос на git commit \- требует approval  
        """  
        *\# Проверить protected branch*  
        if self.\_is\_protected\_branch():  
            return GitResult(  
                success\=False,  
                operation\=GitOperation.COMMIT,  
                output\="",  
                error\=f"Cannot commit to protected branch: {self.\_get\_current\_branch()}"  
            )  
          
        *\# Получить staged changes для preview*  
        \_, diff\_preview, \_ \= self.\_run\_git(\["diff", "--staged"\])  
          
        if not diff\_preview.strip():  
            return GitResult(  
                success\=False,  
                operation\=GitOperation.COMMIT,  
                output\="",  
                error\="Nothing staged to commit. Use 'add' first."  
            )  
          
        approval\_id \= f"commit\_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d\_%H%M%S')}\_{agent\_id}"  
          
        self.\_pending\_approvals\[approval\_id\] \= PendingApproval(  
            id\=approval\_id,  
            operation\=GitOperation.COMMIT,  
            args\={"message": message},  
            diff\_preview\=diff\_preview,  
            created\_at\=datetime.now(),  
            agent\_id\=agent\_id,  
            expires\_at\=datetime.now()  
        )  
          
        return GitResult(  
            success\=True,  
            operation\=GitOperation.COMMIT,  
            output\=f"Approval requested for commit: {message\[:50\]}...",  
            needs\_approval\=True,  
            approval\_id\=approval\_id  
        )  
      
    def request\_push(self, agent\_id: str, branch: Optional\[str\] \= None) \-\> GitResult:  
        """  
        Запрос на git push \- требует approval  
        """  
        branch \= branch or self.\_get\_current\_branch()  
          
        *\# Проверить protected branch*  
        if branch in PROTECTED\_BRANCHES:  
            return GitResult(  
                success\=False,  
                operation\=GitOperation.PUSH,  
                output\="",  
                error\=f"Cannot push to protected branch: {branch}"  
            )  
          
        *\# Получить unpushed commits*  
        \_, commits, \_ \= self.\_run\_git(\["log", "origin/main..HEAD", "--oneline"\])  
          
        approval\_id \= f"push\_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d\_%H%M%S')}\_{agent\_id}"  
          
        self.\_pending\_approvals\[approval\_id\] \= PendingApproval(  
            id\=approval\_id,  
            operation\=GitOperation.PUSH,  
            args\={"branch": branch},  
            diff\_preview\=commits or "(no unpushed commits)",  
            created\_at\=datetime.now(),  
            agent\_id\=agent\_id,  
            expires\_at\=datetime.now()  
        )  
          
        return GitResult(  
            success\=True,  
            operation\=GitOperation.PUSH,  
            output\=f"Approval requested for push to {branch}",  
            needs\_approval\=True,  
            approval\_id\=approval\_id  
        )  
      
    def create\_agent\_branch(self, branch\_name: str, agent\_id: str) \-\> GitResult:  
        """  
        Создать ветку для агента (agent/branch\_name)  
        Не требует approval \- агенты ДОЛЖНЫ работать в своих ветках  
        """  
        full\_branch \= f"{self.AGENT\_BRANCH\_PREFIX}{branch\_name}"  
          
        code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(\["checkout", "-b", full\_branch\])  
          
        return GitResult(  
            success\=(code \== 0),  
            operation\=GitOperation.CREATE\_BRANCH,  
            output\=f"Created and switched to branch: {full\_branch}",  
            error\=err  
        )  
      
    *\# \==================== APPROVAL EXECUTION \====================*  
      
    def approve(self, approval\_id: str) \-\> GitResult:  
        """Подтвердить и выполнить операцию"""  
          
        if approval\_id not in self.\_pending\_approvals:  
            return GitResult(  
                success\=False,  
                operation\=GitOperation.STATUS,  
                output\="",  
                error\=f"Approval not found: {approval\_id}"  
            )  
          
        pending \= self.\_pending\_approvals.pop(approval\_id)  
          
        *\# Выполнить операцию*  
        if pending.operation \== GitOperation.ADD:  
            files \= pending.args\["files"\]  
            code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(\["add"\] \+ files)  
              
        elif pending.operation \== GitOperation.COMMIT:  
            message \= pending.args\["message"\]  
            code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(\["commit", "-m", message\])  
              
        elif pending.operation \== GitOperation.PUSH:  
            branch \= pending.args\["branch"\]  
            code, out, err \= self.\_run\_git(\["push", "origin", branch\])  
              
        else:  
            return GitResult(  
                success\=False,  
                operation\=pending.operation,  
                output\="",  
                error\=f"Unknown operation: {pending.operation}"  
            )  
          
        return GitResult(  
            success\=(code \== 0),  
            operation\=pending.operation,  
            output\=out,  
            error\=err  
        )  
      
    def reject(self, approval\_id: str) \-\> GitResult:  
        """Отклонить операцию"""  
          
        if approval\_id not in self.\_pending\_approvals:  
            return GitResult(  
                success\=False,  
                operation\=GitOperation.STATUS,  
                output\="",  
                error\=f"Approval not found: {approval\_id}"  
            )  
          
        pending \= self.\_pending\_approvals.pop(approval\_id)  
          
        return GitResult(  
            success\=True,  
            operation\=pending.operation,  
            output\=f"Rejected {pending.operation.value} by {pending.agent\_id}"  
        )  
      
    def get\_pending\_approvals(self) \-\> List\[Dict\[str, Any\]\]:  
        """Получить все ожидающие approvals"""  
        return \[  
            {  
                "id": p.id,  
                "operation": p.operation.value,  
                "agent\_id": p.agent\_id,  
                "diff\_preview": p.diff\_preview\[:500\],  *\# Limit preview*  
                "created\_at": p.created\_at.isoformat()  
            }  
            for p in self.\_pending\_approvals.values()  
        \]

*\# Singleton*  
\_git\_tool: Optional\[GitTool\] \= None

def get\_git\_tool() \-\> GitTool:  
    global \_git\_tool  
    if \_git\_tool is None:  
        \_git\_tool \= GitTool()

    return \_git\_tool

---

## **🔧 PHASE 20-C: APPROVAL MANAGER**

### **Файл: `src/tools/approval_manager.py`**

python  
"""  
VETKA Phase 20: Approval Manager  
Centralized approval flow for dangerous operations  
"""

import asyncio  
from datetime import datetime, timedelta  
from typing import Dict, Optional, Callable, Any  
from dataclasses import dataclass  
from enum import Enum  
import uuid

class ApprovalType(Enum):  
    GIT\_ADD \= "git\_add"  
    GIT\_COMMIT \= "git\_commit"  
    GIT\_PUSH \= "git\_push"  
    FILE\_WRITE \= "file\_write"  
    FILE\_DELETE \= "file\_delete"  
    CODE\_EXECUTE \= "code\_execute"

class ApprovalStatus(Enum):  
    PENDING \= "pending"  
    APPROVED \= "approved"  
    REJECTED \= "rejected"  
    EXPIRED \= "expired"

@dataclass  
class ApprovalRequest:  
    id: str  
    type: ApprovalType  
    agent\_id: str  
    description: str  
    diff\_preview: str  
    metadata: Dict\[str, Any\]  
    status: ApprovalStatus  
    created\_at: datetime  
    expires\_at: datetime  
    resolved\_at: Optional\[datetime\] \= None  
    resolved\_by: Optional\[str\] \= None

class ApprovalManager:  
    """  
    Централизованный менеджер approvals  
      
    Features:  
    \- Timeout (auto-reject после 120s)  
    \- Socket.IO интеграция  
    \- История approvals  
    """  
      
    DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT \= 120  *\# seconds*  
      
    def \_\_init\_\_(self, socketio\=None):  
        self.\_requests: Dict\[str, ApprovalRequest\] \= {}  
        self.\_history: list\[ApprovalRequest\] \= \[\]  
        self.\_socketio \= socketio  
        self.\_callbacks: Dict\[str, Callable\] \= {}  
      
    def set\_socketio(self, socketio):  
        """Установить Socket.IO instance"""  
        self.\_socketio \= socketio  
      
    def create\_request(  
        self,  
        type: ApprovalType,  
        agent\_id: str,  
        description: str,  
        diff\_preview: str \= "",  
        metadata: Optional\[Dict\[str, Any\]\] \= None,  
        timeout: int \= DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT,  
        on\_approved: Optional\[Callable\] \= None,  
        on\_rejected: Optional\[Callable\] \= None  
    ) \-\> ApprovalRequest:  
        """  
        Создать запрос на approval  
          
        Args:  
            type: Тип операции  
            agent\_id: ID агента  
            description: Описание операции  
            diff\_preview: Превью изменений (diff)  
            metadata: Дополнительные данные  
            timeout: Таймаут в секундах  
            on\_approved: Callback при approve  
            on\_rejected: Callback при reject  
          
        Returns:  
            ApprovalRequest  
        """  
        request\_id \= f"{type.value}\_{uuid.uuid4().hex\[:8\]}"  
        now \= datetime.now()  
          
        request \= ApprovalRequest(  
            id\=request\_id,  
            type\=type,  
            agent\_id\=agent\_id,  
            description\=description,  
            diff\_preview\=diff\_preview,  
            metadata\=metadata or {},  
            status\=ApprovalStatus.PENDING,  
            created\_at\=now,  
            expires\_at\=now \+ timedelta(seconds\=timeout)  
        )  
          
        self.\_requests\[request\_id\] \= request  
          
        *\# Сохранить callbacks*  
        if on\_approved:  
            self.\_callbacks\[f"{request\_id}\_approved"\] \= on\_approved  
        if on\_rejected:  
            self.\_callbacks\[f"{request\_id}\_rejected"\] \= on\_rejected  
          
        *\# Отправить в UI через Socket.IO*  
        self.\_emit\_approval\_needed(request)  
          
        *\# Запустить таймер*  
        asyncio.create\_task(self.\_start\_timeout(request\_id, timeout))  
          
        return request  
      
    async def \_start\_timeout(self, request\_id: str, timeout: int):  
        """Таймер для auto-reject"""  
        await asyncio.sleep(timeout)  
          
        if request\_id in self.\_requests:  
            request \= self.\_requests\[request\_id\]  
            if request.status \== ApprovalStatus.PENDING:  
                self.\_expire\_request(request\_id)  
      
    def \_expire\_request(self, request\_id: str):  
        """Истечь request по таймауту"""  
        if request\_id not in self.\_requests:  
            return  
          
        request \= self.\_requests\[request\_id\]  
        request.status \= ApprovalStatus.EXPIRED  
        request.resolved\_at \= datetime.now()  
          
        *\# Переместить в историю*  
        self.\_history.append(request)  
        del self.\_requests\[request\_id\]  
          
        *\# Вызвать reject callback*  
        callback\_key \= f"{request\_id}\_rejected"  
        if callback\_key in self.\_callbacks:  
            self.\_callbacks\[callback\_key\]("Timeout \- auto-rejected")  
            del self.\_callbacks\[callback\_key\]  
          
        *\# Уведомить UI*  
        self.\_emit\_approval\_resolved(request)  
      
    def approve(self, request\_id: str, user\_id: str \= "human") \-\> bool:  
        """Подтвердить request"""  
        if request\_id not in self.\_requests:  
            return False  
          
        request \= self.\_requests\[request\_id\]  
          
        if request.status \!= ApprovalStatus.PENDING:  
            return False  
          
        request.status \= ApprovalStatus.APPROVED  
        request.resolved\_at \= datetime.now()  
        request.resolved\_by \= user\_id  
          
        *\# Переместить в историю*  
        self.\_history.append(request)  
        del self.\_requests\[request\_id\]  
          
        *\# Вызвать callback*  
        callback\_key \= f"{request\_id}\_approved"  
        if callback\_key in self.\_callbacks:  
            self.\_callbacks\[callback\_key\]()  
            del self.\_callbacks\[callback\_key\]  
          
        *\# Уведомить UI*  
        self.\_emit\_approval\_resolved(request)  
          
        return True  
      
    def reject(self, request\_id: str, user\_id: str \= "human", reason: str \= "") \-\> bool:  
        """Отклонить request"""  
        if request\_id not in self.\_requests:  
            return False  
          
        request \= self.\_requests\[request\_id\]  
          
        if request.status \!= ApprovalStatus.PENDING:  
            return False  
          
        request.status \= ApprovalStatus.REJECTED  
        request.resolved\_at \= datetime.now()  
        request.resolved\_by \= user\_id  
        request.metadata\["reject\_reason"\] \= reason  
          
        *\# Переместить в историю*  
        self.\_history.append(request)  
        del self.\_requests\[request\_id\]  
          
        *\# Вызвать callback*  
        callback\_key \= f"{request\_id}\_rejected"  
        if callback\_key in self.\_callbacks:  
            self.\_callbacks\[callback\_key\](reason)  
            del self.\_callbacks\[callback\_key\]  
          
        *\# Уведомить UI*  
        self.\_emit\_approval\_resolved(request)  
          
        return True  
      
    def get\_pending(self) \-\> list\[Dict\[str, Any\]\]:  
        """Получить все pending requests"""  
        return \[  
            {  
                "id": r.id,  
                "type": r.type.value,  
                "agent\_id": r.agent\_id,  
                "description": r.description,  
                "diff\_preview": r.diff\_preview\[:1000\],  *\# Limit*  
                "created\_at": r.created\_at.isoformat(),  
                "expires\_in": (r.expires\_at \- datetime.now()).total\_seconds()  
            }  
            for r in self.\_requests.values()  
            if r.status \== ApprovalStatus.PENDING  
        \]  
      
    def get\_history(self, limit: int \= 50) \-\> list\[Dict\[str, Any\]\]:  
        """Получить историю approvals"""  
        return \[  
            {  
                "id": r.id,  
                "type": r.type.value,  
                "agent\_id": r.agent\_id,  
                "description": r.description,  
                "status": r.status.value,  
                "resolved\_by": r.resolved\_by,  
                "created\_at": r.created\_at.isoformat(),  
                "resolved\_at": r.resolved\_at.isoformat() if r.resolved\_at else None  
            }  
            for r in self.\_history\[\-limit:\]  
        \]  
      
    *\# \==================== Socket.IO Integration \====================*  
      
    def \_emit\_approval\_needed(self, request: ApprovalRequest):  
        """Отправить событие в UI"""  
        if self.\_socketio:  
            self.\_socketio.emit('approval\_needed', {  
                "id": request.id,  
                "type": request.type.value,  
                "agent\_id": request.agent\_id,  
                "description": request.description,  
                "diff\_preview": request.diff\_preview,  
                "expires\_in": self.DEFAULT\_TIMEOUT  
            })  
      
    def \_emit\_approval\_resolved(self, request: ApprovalRequest):  
        """Отправить событие о resolve"""  
        if self.\_socketio:  
            self.\_socketio.emit('approval\_resolved', {  
                "id": request.id,  
                "status": request.status.value,  
                "resolved\_by": request.resolved\_by  
            })

*\# Singleton*  
\_approval\_manager: Optional\[ApprovalManager\] \= None

def get\_approval\_manager() \-\> ApprovalManager:  
    global \_approval\_manager  
    if \_approval\_manager is None:  
        \_approval\_manager \= ApprovalManager()

    return \_approval\_manager

## **🔧 PHASE 20-D: APPROVAL MODAL (Frontend)**

### **Файл: `static/js/approval_modal.js`**

javascript  
*/\*\**  
 \* VETKA Phase 20: Approval Modal  
 \* UI component for approve/reject dangerous operations  
 *\*/*

class ApprovalModal {  
    constructor(socketInstance) {  
        this.socket \= socketInstance;  
        this.pendingApprovals \= new Map();  
        this.modalContainer \= null;  
          
        this.\_init();  
        this.\_bindSocketEvents();  
    }  
      
    \_init() {  
        *// Создать контейнер для модалей*  
        this.modalContainer \= document.createElement('div');  
        this.modalContainer.id \= 'approval-modal-container';  
        this.modalContainer.innerHTML \= \`  
            \<style\>  
                .approval-overlay {  
                    position: fixed;  
                    top: 0;  
                    left: 0;  
                    right: 0;  
                    bottom: 0;  
                    background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.7);  
                    display: flex;  
                    align-items: center;  
                    justify-content: center;  
                    z-index: 10000;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-modal {  
                    background: \#1e1e2e;  
                    border: 1px solid \#45475a;  
                    border-radius: 12px;  
                    width: 90%;  
                    max-width: 700px;  
                    max-height: 80vh;  
                    overflow: hidden;  
                    display: flex;  
                    flex-direction: column;  
                    box-shadow: 0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);  
                }  
                  
                .approval-header {  
                    padding: 16px 20px;  
                    background: \#313244;  
                    border-bottom: 1px solid \#45475a;  
                    display: flex;  
                    align-items: center;  
                    justify-content: space-between;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-header h3 {  
                    margin: 0;  
                    color: \#cdd6f4;  
                    font-size: 16px;  
                    display: flex;  
                    align-items: center;  
                    gap: 8px;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-type-badge {  
                    padding: 4px 8px;  
                    border-radius: 4px;  
                    font-size: 12px;  
                    font-weight: 600;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-type-badge.git\_commit { background: \#f9e2af; color: \#1e1e2e; }  
                .approval-type-badge.git\_push { background: \#f38ba8; color: \#1e1e2e; }  
                .approval-type-badge.git\_add { background: \#a6e3a1; color: \#1e1e2e; }  
                .approval-type-badge.file\_write { background: \#89b4fa; color: \#1e1e2e; }  
                .approval-type-badge.code\_execute { background: \#cba6f7; color: \#1e1e2e; }  
                  
                .approval-timer {  
                    color: \#f38ba8;  
                    font-size: 14px;  
                    font-weight: 600;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-body {  
                    padding: 20px;  
                    overflow-y: auto;  
                    flex: 1;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-description {  
                    color: \#cdd6f4;  
                    margin-bottom: 16px;  
                    font-size: 14px;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-agent {  
                    color: \#6c7086;  
                    font-size: 12px;  
                    margin-bottom: 12px;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-diff {  
                    background: \#11111b;  
                    border: 1px solid \#45475a;  
                    border-radius: 8px;  
                    padding: 12px;  
                    font-family: 'JetBrains Mono', monospace;  
                    font-size: 12px;  
                    overflow-x: auto;  
                    max-height: 300px;  
                    overflow-y: auto;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-diff .diff-add { color: \#a6e3a1; }  
                .approval-diff .diff-remove { color: \#f38ba8; }  
                .approval-diff .diff-header { color: \#89b4fa; }  
                  
                .approval-footer {  
                    padding: 16px 20px;  
                    background: \#313244;  
                    border-top: 1px solid \#45475a;  
                    display: flex;  
                    justify-content: flex-end;  
                    gap: 12px;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-btn {  
                    padding: 10px 24px;  
                    border-radius: 8px;  
                    border: none;  
                    font-size: 14px;  
                    font-weight: 600;  
                    cursor: pointer;  
                    transition: all 0.2s;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-btn-approve {  
                    background: \#a6e3a1;  
                    color: \#1e1e2e;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-btn-approve:hover {  
                    background: \#94e2a5;  
                    transform: translateY(-1px);  
                }  
                  
                .approval-btn-reject {  
                    background: \#45475a;  
                    color: \#cdd6f4;  
                }  
                  
                .approval-btn-reject:hover {  
                    background: \#f38ba8;  
                    color: \#1e1e2e;  
                }  
            \</style\>  
        \`;  
        document.body.appendChild(this.modalContainer);  
    }  
      
    \_bindSocketEvents() {  
        *// Новый approval request*  
        this.socket.on('approval\_needed', (data) \=\> {  
            console.log('\[Approval\] New request:', data);  
            this.\_showModal(data);  
        });  
          
        *// Approval resolved (от другого клиента или timeout)*  
        this.socket.on('approval\_resolved', (data) \=\> {  
            console.log('\[Approval\] Resolved:', data);  
            this.\_closeModal(data.id);  
        });  
    }  
      
    \_showModal(data) {  
        const { id, type, agent\_id, description, diff\_preview, expires\_in } \= data;  
          
        *// Форматировать diff*  
        const formattedDiff \= this.\_formatDiff(diff\_preview);  
          
        const modal \= document.createElement('div');  
        modal.className \= 'approval-overlay';  
        modal.id \= \`approval-${id}\`;  
        modal.innerHTML \= \`  
            \<div class="approval-modal"\>  
                \<div class="approval-header"\>  
                    \<h3\>  
                        \<span class="approval-type-badge ${type}"\>${type.replace('\_', ' ').toUpperCase()}\</span\>  
                        Approval Required  
                    \</h3\>  
                    \<span class="approval-timer" id="timer-${id}"\>${expires\_in}s\</span\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<div class="approval-body"\>  
                    \<div class="approval-agent"\>Agent: \<strong\>${agent\_id}\</strong\>\</div\>  
                    \<div class="approval-description"\>${description}\</div\>  
                    \<div class="approval-diff"\>${formattedDiff}\</div\>  
                \</div\>  
                \<div class="approval-footer"\>  
                    \<button class="approval-btn approval-btn-reject" onclick="approvalModal.reject('${id}')"\>  
                        ✕ Reject  
                    \</button\>  
                    \<button class="approval-btn approval-btn-approve" onclick="approvalModal.approve('${id}')"\>  
                        ✓ Approve  
                    \</button\>  
                \</div\>  
            \</div\>  
        \`;  
          
        this.modalContainer.appendChild(modal);  
        this.pendingApprovals.set(id, { modal, expiresIn: expires\_in });  
          
        *// Запустить таймер*  
        this.\_startTimer(id, expires\_in);  
    }  
      
    \_formatDiff(diff) {  
        if (\!diff) return '\<span style="color: \#6c7086"\>(no changes to preview)\</span\>';  
          
        return diff  
            .split('\\n')  
            .map(line \=\> {  
                if (line.startsWith('+') && \!line.startsWith('+++')) {  
                    return \`\<span class="diff-add"\>${this.\_escapeHtml(line)}\</span\>\`;  
                } else if (line.startsWith('-') && \!line.startsWith('---')) {  
                    return \`\<span class="diff-remove"\>${this.\_escapeHtml(line)}\</span\>\`;  
                } else if (line.startsWith('@@') || line.startsWith('diff') || line.startsWith('index')) {  
                    return \`\<span class="diff-header"\>${this.\_escapeHtml(line)}\</span\>\`;  
                }  
                return this.\_escapeHtml(line);  
            })  
            .join('\\n');  
    }  
      
    \_escapeHtml(text) {  
        const div \= document.createElement('div');  
        div.textContent \= text;  
        return div.innerHTML;  
    }  
      
    \_startTimer(id, seconds) {  
        const timerEl \= document.getElementById(\`timer-${id}\`);  
        if (\!timerEl) return;  
          
        let remaining \= seconds;  
          
        const interval \= setInterval(() \=\> {  
            remaining\--;  
            timerEl.textContent \= \`${remaining}s\`;  
              
            if (remaining \<= 10) {  
                timerEl.style.animation \= 'pulse 0.5s infinite';  
            }  
              
            if (remaining \<= 0) {  
                clearInterval(interval);  
                this.\_closeModal(id);  
            }  
        }, 1000);  
          
        *// Сохранить interval для cleanup*  
        const approval \= this.pendingApprovals.get(id);  
        if (approval) {  
            approval.interval \= interval;  
        }  
    }  
      
    \_closeModal(id) {  
        const approval \= this.pendingApprovals.get(id);  
        if (approval) {  
            if (approval.interval) {  
                clearInterval(approval.interval);  
            }  
            approval.modal.remove();  
            this.pendingApprovals.delete(id);  
        }  
    }  
      
    approve(id) {  
        console.log('\[Approval\] Approving:', id);  
        this.socket.emit('approval\_response', { id, approved: true });  
        this.\_closeModal(id);  
    }  
      
    reject(id) {  
        console.log('\[Approval\] Rejecting:', id);  
        this.socket.emit('approval\_response', { id, approved: false });  
        this.\_closeModal(id);  
    }  
}

*// Global instance*  
let approvalModal \= null;

function initApprovalModal(socket) {  
    approvalModal \= new ApprovalModal(socket);  
    console.log('\[Approval\] Modal initialized');  
    return approvalModal;

}

## **🔧 PHASE 20-E: API ROUTES**

### **Файл: `src/server/routes/approval_routes.py`**

python  
"""  
VETKA Phase 20: Approval API Routes  
"""

from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify  
from src.tools.approval\_manager import get\_approval\_manager  
from src.tools.git\_tool import get\_git\_tool

approval\_bp \= Blueprint('approval', \_\_name\_\_, url\_prefix\='/api/approval')

@approval\_bp.route('/pending', methods\=\['GET'\])  
def get\_pending\_approvals():  
    """Получить все pending approvals"""  
    manager \= get\_approval\_manager()  
    return jsonify({  
        "success": True,  
        "approvals": manager.get\_pending()  
    })

@approval\_bp.route('/history', methods\=\['GET'\])  
def get\_approval\_history():  
    """Получить историю approvals"""  
    limit \= request.args.get('limit', 50, type\=int)  
    manager \= get\_approval\_manager()  
    return jsonify({  
        "success": True,  
        "history": manager.get\_history(limit)  
    })

@approval\_bp.route('/approve/\<approval\_id\>', methods\=\['POST'\])  
def approve\_request(approval\_id):  
    """Подтвердить approval"""  
    user\_id \= request.json.get('user\_id', 'human')  
    manager \= get\_approval\_manager()  
      
    success \= manager.approve(approval\_id, user\_id)  
      
    if success:  
        return jsonify({"success": True, "message": f"Approved: {approval\_id}"})  
    else:  
        return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "Approval not found or already resolved"}), 404

@approval\_bp.route('/reject/\<approval\_id\>', methods\=\['POST'\])  
def reject\_request(approval\_id):  
    """Отклонить approval"""  
    user\_id \= request.json.get('user\_id', 'human')  
    reason \= request.json.get('reason', '')  
    manager \= get\_approval\_manager()  
      
    success \= manager.reject(approval\_id, user\_id, reason)  
      
    if success:  
        return jsonify({"success": True, "message": f"Rejected: {approval\_id}"})  
    else:  
        return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "Approval not found or already resolved"}), 404

*\# Git-specific routes*  
@approval\_bp.route('/git/status', methods\=\['GET'\])  
def git\_status():  
    """Git status (no approval needed)"""  
    git \= get\_git\_tool()  
    result \= git.status()  
    return jsonify({  
        "success": result.success,  
        "output": result.output,  
        "error": result.error  
    })

@approval\_bp.route('/git/diff', methods\=\['GET'\])  
def git\_diff():  
    """Git diff (no approval needed)"""  
    staged \= request.args.get('staged', 'false').lower() \== 'true'  
    file\_path \= request.args.get('file')  
      
    git \= get\_git\_tool()  
    result \= git.diff(staged\=staged, file\_path\=file\_path)  
    return jsonify({  
        "success": result.success,  
        "output": result.output,  
        "error": result.error

    })

## **✅ ТЕСТЫ**

### **Файл: `tests/test_phase_20/test_sandbox.py`**

python  
"""Tests for Phase 20 Sandbox Executor"""

import pytest  
from src.tools.sandbox\_executor import SandboxExecutor, SandboxLevel

class TestSandboxExecutor:  
      
    @pytest.fixture  
    def executor(self):  
        return SandboxExecutor()  
      
    def test\_simple\_execution(self, executor):  
        """Test basic code execution"""  
        result \= executor.execute("print('Hello, VETKA\!')")  
        assert result.success  
        assert "Hello, VETKA\!" in result.stdout  
      
    def test\_network\_blocked(self, executor):  
        """Test that network is blocked"""  
        code \= """  
import urllib.request  
try:  
    urllib.request.urlopen('http://google.com')  
    print('FAIL: Network should be blocked')  
except:  
    print('OK: Network blocked')  
"""  
        result \= executor.execute(code)  
        assert "OK: Network blocked" in result.stdout or not result.success  
      
    def test\_filesystem\_restricted(self, executor):  
        """Test filesystem restrictions"""  
        code \= """  
try:  
    with open('/etc/passwd', 'r') as f:  
        print('FAIL: Should not read /etc/passwd')  
except:  
    print('OK: Filesystem restricted')  
"""  
        result \= executor.execute(code, level\=SandboxLevel.READONLY)  
        assert "OK: Filesystem restricted" in result.stdout or not result.success  
      
    def test\_timeout(self, executor):  
        """Test execution timeout"""  
        code \= "import time; time.sleep(100)"  
        result \= executor.execute(code, timeout\=2)  
        assert not result.success  
        assert "timeout" in result.stderr.lower()  
      
    def test\_sandbox\_tmp\_writable(self, executor):  
        """Test that sandbox tmp is writable"""  
        code \= """  
with open('/tmp/vetka\_sandbox/test.txt', 'w') as f:  
    f.write('test')  
print('OK: Write successful')  
"""  
        result \= executor.execute(code, level\=SandboxLevel.STANDARD)  
        assert result.success

        assert "OK: Write successful" in result.stdout

### **Файл: `tests/test_phase_20/test_git_tool.py`**

python  
"""Tests for Phase 20 Git Tool"""

import pytest  
from src.tools.git\_tool import GitTool, GitOperation, PROTECTED\_BRANCHES

class TestGitTool:  
      
    @pytest.fixture  
    def git(self):  
        return GitTool()  
      
    def test\_status(self, git):  
        """Test git status (safe operation)"""  
        result \= git.status()  
        assert result.success  
        assert result.operation \== GitOperation.STATUS  
        assert not result.needs\_approval  
      
    def test\_diff(self, git):  
        """Test git diff (safe operation)"""  
        result \= git.diff()  
        assert result.success  
        assert result.operation \== GitOperation.DIFF  
      
    def test\_branches(self, git):  
        """Test branch listing"""  
        result \= git.branches()  
        assert result.success  
        assert "main" in result.output or "master" in result.output  
      
    def test\_commit\_needs\_approval(self, git):  
        """Test that commit requires approval"""  
        result \= git.request\_commit("Test commit", "test\_agent")  
        *\# Либо needs\_approval=True, либо error (nothing staged)*  
        assert result.needs\_approval or "Nothing staged" in result.error  
      
    def test\_protected\_branch\_blocked(self, git):  
        """Test that protected branches are blocked"""  
        *\# This test depends on current branch*  
        for branch in PROTECTED\_BRANCHES:  
            *\# Simulating check*  
            assert git.\_is\_protected\_branch(branch)  
      
    def test\_agent\_branch\_creation(self, git):  
        """Test agent branch creation"""  
        result \= git.create\_agent\_branch("test-feature", "test\_agent")  
        *\# May fail if branch exists, but should not require approval*  
        assert not result.needs\_approval

# **🔍 RESEARCH REQUESTS ДЛЯ GROK**

**Дата:** 27 декабря 2025  
 **Цель:** Получить готовые, production-ready решения БЕЗ выдумок

## **ЗАПРОС \#1: Agent Tools Framework (Ready-to-use Libraries)**

### **Контекст**

VETKA \- система визуализации дерева файлов проекта как граф. Чат интегрирован с этим деревом. Агенты (PM, Dev, QA, Deepseek, Grok) должны иметь стандартный набор инструментов для работы с файловой системой и проектом в реальном времени.

**Текущее состояние:**

* Flask backend с Ollama, OpenRouter, Gemini, Grok APIs  
* Агенты общаются через prompt-based routing  
* Нет формального framework для инструментов

**Требования:**

* Инструменты: read\_file, write\_file, search\_code (grep), execute\_bash, git\_status, list\_files  
* Работают локально (не требуют облачные сервисы)  
* Безопасные (sandboxing, permission checks)  
* Интегрируются с Python Flask backend  
* Работают с Ollama \+ OpenRouter LLMs  
* Асинхронные (async/await, не блокирующие)

### **Точный вопрос для Grok:**

"What are the best open-source Python libraries and patterns   
for implementing a production-ready Agent Tools framework in December 2025?

Context:  
\- Flask REST API backend  
\- Multiple LLM providers (Ollama local, OpenRouter API, Gemini, Grok)  
\- Tools needed: file operations (read/write), code search (grep),   
  bash execution, git integration, filesystem listing  
\- Must be async-safe for Socket.IO real-time updates  
\- Security: no arbitrary code execution, sandboxed filesystem access  
\- Integration: Tools called by LLM agents via function calling

Provide:  
1\. Top 3-5 most maintained Python libraries for agent tools   
   (e.g., LangChain Tools, Anthropic Tools SDK, AutoGen tools, etc.)  
2\. Comparison table: features, security, async support, local-first  
3\. Concrete code example: How to implement read\_file \+ search\_code tools  
   with proper error handling  
4\. Integration pattern: How to pass tools to Ollama/OpenRouter calls  
5\. Security best practices: sandboxing, permission checks, examples  
6\. Any gotchas or common mistakes in December 2025

Make it battle-tested, no experimental features."

### **Ожидаемый результат:**

* Конкретные библиотеки с npm/pip ссылками  
* Рабочий пример (150-200 строк)  
* Security checklist  
* Async patterns

---

## **ЗАПРОС \#2: Chat Persistence in Triple Write (Qdrant \+ Weaviate)**

### **Контекст**

VETKA использует **Triple Write Architecture**:

* **Qdrant** (512D vectors, semantic search)  
* **Weaviate** (graph relationships, structured metadata)  
* **ChangeLog** (immutable JSON audit trail)

Чаты должны сохраняться в этой системе **привязанные к узлам дерева** (файлам):

User clicks: /src/main.py (node\_id \= "abc123")  
Chat opens → User talks to agent  
Agent responds → Chat saved as:  
{  
  "chat\_id": "chat\_xyz789",  
  "node\_id": "abc123",           ← привязка к файлу\!  
  "file\_path": "/src/main.py",  
  "timestamp": 1735308000,  
  "messages": \[  
    {"role": "user", "content": "fix bug", "reaction": "👍"},  
    {"role": "agent", "content": "found it...", "agent\_type": "dev"}  
  \],  
  "embedding\_text": "combined conversation for vector search",  
  "metadata": {  
    "knowledge\_level": 0.45,  
    "surprise\_metric": 0.72,  
    "agent\_responses": 3,  
    "artifacts\_created": 1  
  }  
}

**Текущее состояние:**

* Qdrant: 768D embeddings (Gemma 2), 513 документов  
* Weaviate: VetkaLeaf collection для файлов  
* ChangeLog: JSON логи в data/  
* Чаты: ТОЛЬКО в памяти браузера (теряются при перезагрузке\!)

**Требования:**

* Сохранять каждый чат в Qdrant с embedding  
* Семантические связи в Weaviate (chat → related files)  
* Immutable запись в ChangeLog  
* Быстрый retrieval: "все чаты для файла X"  
* Обновляемые reactions (👍👎⭐)  
* Graceful degradation (работает если 1-2 хранилища down)

### **Точный вопрос для Grok:**

"How to implement chat persistence with Triple Write architecture   
(Qdrant \+ Weaviate \+ JSON ChangeLog) in Python Flask, December 2025?

Architecture:  
\- Qdrant: 768D embeddings, FAISS/HNSW index  
\- Weaviate: GraphQL API, schema-based relationships  
\- ChangeLog: Append-only JSON files

Requirements:  
1\. Save chat conversations with embeddings in Qdrant  
2\. Store relationships in Weaviate (chat → related\_files)  
3\. Immutable audit trail in JSON ChangeLog  
4\. Chat indexed by: node\_id, file\_path, timestamp  
5\. Support reactions (emoji buttons) as updatable metadata  
6\. Fast retrieval: Find all chats for a given file  
7\. Graceful degradation: Works if 1-2 backends unavailable  
8\. Async operations (don't block Socket.IO)

Provide:  
1\. Data schema design for Qdrant and Weaviate  
2\. Python code: ChatPersistenceManager class (async methods)  
   \- save\_chat(chat\_data) → returns chat\_id  
   \- get\_chats\_for\_file(node\_id) → returns \[chats\]  
   \- update\_reaction(chat\_id, message\_id, emoji, active)  
   \- search\_chats(query) → semantic search across all chats  
3\. Integration with Flask routes (Flask-SQLAlchemy style)  
4\. Error handling and retry logic  
5\. Migration strategy from in-memory to persistent  
6\. Query examples for common operations

Focus on battle-tested patterns, not experimental."

### **Ожидаемый результат:**

* Schema.json для Qdrant/Weaviate  
* ChatPersistenceManager class (200-300 строк)  
* Flask route examples  
* Migration script  
* Query examples

## **ЗАПРОС \#3: Streaming Responses (WebSocket \+ Server-Sent Events)**

### **Контекст**

Текущая проблема:

User types: "@deepseek analyze this code"  
↓ 5-10 секунд ОЖИДАНИЯ...  
↓ Вся ответ появляется СРАЗУ

Нужно:  
User types: "@deepseek analyze this code"  
↓ Агент начинает печатать  
↓ "I found several issues... \[chunk 1\]"  
↓ "The main problem is... \[chunk 2\]"    
↓ "Here's the fix... \[chunk 3\]"  
↓ Полный ответ за 2-3 сек вместо 10

**Текущее состояние:**

* Flask \+ Socket.IO, Socket.IO broadcasts работают  
* Все LLM responses ждут до конца (blocking)  
* No streaming поддержки

**Требования:**

* Стриминг от Ollama (llama3.2, qwen2.5)  
* Стриминг от OpenRouter (claude, gpt-4, deepseek)  
* Стриминг от Gemini API  
* Graceful fallback если LLM не поддерживает streaming  
* "Agent typing..." indicator  
* Cancel ability (user может остановить)  
* Работает через Socket.IO (не требует отдельный WebSocket)

### **Точный вопрос для Grok:**

"Best practices for implementing LLM streaming responses   
in Flask \+ Socket.IO architecture, December 2025?

Setup:  
\- Flask backend with Socket.IO for real-time updates  
\- Multiple LLM providers:  
  \* Ollama (local, /api/generate endpoint)  
  \* OpenRouter (API, supports streaming)  
  \* Gemini API (supports streaming)  
\- Need to stream responses to browser in real-time  
\- Show 'Agent typing...' indicator while streaming  
\- Support cancellation mid-stream

Requirements:  
1\. Stream tokens as they arrive from LLM  
2\. Emit Socket.IO events for each chunk  
3\. Browser receives chunks and appends to DOM  
4\. Fallback: if LLM doesn't support streaming, batch send  
5\. Error handling: truncate if stream breaks  
6\. Support for structured responses (JSON, markdown, code)  
7\. Async/await, non-blocking operations  
8\. Memory efficient (no accumulate entire response)

Provide:  
1\. Backend code: async streaming wrapper for each LLM provider  
2\. Socket.IO message protocol (what format to send chunks)  
3\. Frontend JavaScript: receive chunks, render in real-time  
4\. Example: Full end-to-end streaming with Ollama \+ Socket.IO  
5\. Comparison: Stream vs batch performance metrics  
6\. Gotchas and optimization tips  
7\. How to integrate with existing Flask+SocketIO app

Focus on production patterns that work in December 2025,  
not experimental or bleeding-edge approaches."

### **Ожидаемый результат:**

* Backend streaming wrapper class (150-200 строк)  
* Socket.IO protocol specification  
* Frontend JavaScript (100-150 строк)  
* Working example (Ollama streaming)  
* Fallback logic  
* Performance metrics
